## Brazil

**Gonzaga, Chiquinha (1847–1935)**

Brazilian composer, pianist, and conductor; a central figure in early choro and Brazilian theatrical music with many piano works.

**Chaminade, Cécile (1857–1944)**

French composer and pianist; published extensively and gained international popularity for her piano music and songs.

**Bonis, Mel (1858–1937)**

French composer and pianist (Mélanie Bonis); published a large output including many solo piano pieces.

- Links: [Wikipedia](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mel_Bonis) · [IMSLP](https://imslp.org/wiki/Category:Bonis,_Mel) · [Wikidata](https://www.wikidata.org/wiki/Q467452)

**Schumann, Clara (1819–1896)**

German pianist, composer, and piano teacher; among the most distinguished concert pianists of the Romantic era.

**Beach, Amy (1867–1944)**

American composer and pianist; among the first American women to achieve major success as a composer of large-scale art music.

## Venezuela

**Carreño, Teresa (1853–1917)**

Venezuelan pianist, composer, soprano, and conductor; an internationally renowned virtuoso often dubbed the “Valkyrie of the Piano”.
